	<body>
		<category name="BL2 Hybrids">
			<category name="Description">
				<comment>50 pieces of gear await for you to claim for your own. Any item that can be a hybrid has a roughly 1-in-100 chance of spawning as a hybrid.</comment>
				<comment>Some mod guns can be hybrids too! As long as the gun replacer in question replaces a Legendary weapon (excluding the Norfleet and DLC Legendaries), it should hybrid-ify pretty well. If your gun replaces a non-Legendary, you would need to manually adjust it if you want it to hybrid.</comment>
				<comment>Hybrid Uniques will be Legendary rarity. Hybrid Seraphs and Hybrid Pearls will be Effervescent (rainbow) rarity. </comment>
				<comment>A few seraphs and pearls had their rarity adjusted so that their hybrids will spawn in rainbow rarity instead of a white rarity. Keep this in mind if you use a mod that alters the rarity system.</comment>
				<comment>Cracked Sash was also adjusted like the seraphs and pearls, but just so that the hybrid will spawn as legendary.</comment>
				<comment>The Infinity was altered so that it should work properly with the normal Double pistol accessory. Disable it if you use a mod that replaces the Infinity.</comment>
				<comment>The folder below lists what can spawn as a hybrid, and the folder below that one lists the specific hybrids (along with some dumb nicknames for the hell of it).</comment>
				<category name="Gear that is hybridized">

				<category name="Basic guide to making something hybridizable">
					<comment>This is assuming you have a basic knowledge of BL2 modding.</comment>
					<comment>1. Set the gun you want to be hybridizable to be able to spawn the part. You'll need to find the weaponpartlistcollectiondefinition (or itempartlistcollectiondefinition, if it is a shield), which can be found relatively easily by opening up the console in borderlands 2 and typing "getall willowgame.weaponpartlistcollectiondefinition name" and hitting enter. An example of a gun being enabled to spawn with another barrel is at the bottom of this file.</comment>
					<category name="Example of a gun set to spawn with another barrel">
						<comment>#set GD_Weap_Pistol.A_Weapons_Unique.Pistol_Dahl_3_Teapot:WeaponPartListCollectionDefinition_110 BarrelPartData</comment>
						<comment>(</comment>
						<comment>    bEnabled = True,</comment>
						<comment>    WeightedParts =</comment>
						<comment>    (</comment>
						<comment>        (</comment>
						<comment>            Part = WeaponPartDefinition'GD_Weap_Pistol.Barrel.Pistol_Barrel_Tediore_Teapot',</comment>
						<comment>            Manufacturers =</comment>
						<comment>            (</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = None,</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 1</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Bandit',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 1</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Dahl',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 1</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Hyperion',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 1</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Jakobs',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 1</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Maliwan',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 1</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Tediore',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 1</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Torgue',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 1</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Vladof',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 1</comment>
						<comment>                )</comment>
						<comment>            ),</comment>
						<comment>            MinGameStageIndex = 0,</comment>
						<comment>            MaxGameStageIndex = 1,</comment>
						<comment>            DefaultWeightIndex = 1</comment>
						<comment>        ),</comment>
						<comment>        (</comment>
						<comment>            Part = WeaponPartDefinition'GD_Weap_Pistol.Barrel.Pistol_Barrel_Dahl_Hornet',</comment>
						<comment>            Manufacturers =</comment>
						<comment>            (</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = None,</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 0</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Bandit',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 0</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Dahl',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 0</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Hyperion',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 0</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Jakobs',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 0</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Maliwan',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 0</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Tediore',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 0</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Torgue',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 0</comment>
						<comment>                ),</comment>
						<comment>                (</comment>
						<comment>                    Manufacturer = ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Vladof',</comment>
						<comment>                    DefaultWeightIndex = 0</comment>
						<comment>                )</comment>
						<comment>            ),</comment>
						<comment>            MinGameStageIndex = 0,</comment>
						<comment>            MaxGameStageIndex = 1,</comment>
						<comment>            DefaultWeightIndex = 0</comment>
						<comment>        )</comment>
						<comment>    )</comment>
						<comment>)</comment>
					</category>
					<comment>2. Put the stats and/or behaviors on the meterial of the gun. Firing Modes don't work when put on a material.</comment>
					<comment>I usually compare the barrel to the "vanilla" version, like the Fremington's Edge's barrel compared to the normal Hyperion barrel.</comment>
					<comment>Then I take whatever the special gun changed extra to the normal gun barrel and put it on the material.</comment>
					<comment>So if the normal barrel boosted damage by 10%, and Fremington boosted damage by 20%, I'd take that extra 10% and put in on the material.</comment>
					<comment>------</comment>
					<comment>Shields are pretty similar, but you'll want to put the stats and behaviors on the accessory instead of the material.</comment>
				</category>
			</category>

(bEnabled=True,WeightedParts=((Part=WeaponPartDefinition'GD_Weap_Pistol.Barrel.Pistol_Barrel_Tediore_Teapot',Manufacturers=((Manufacturer=None,DefaultWeightIndex=1),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Bandit',DefaultWeightIndex=1),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Dahl',DefaultWeightIndex=1),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Hyperion',DefaultWeightIndex=1),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Jakobs',DefaultWeightIndex=1),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Maliwan',DefaultWeightIndex=1),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Tediore',DefaultWeightIndex=1),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Torgue',DefaultWeightIndex=1),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Vladof',DefaultWeightIndex=1)),MinGameStageIndex=0,MaxGameStageIndex=1,DefaultWeightIndex=1),(Part=WeaponPartDefinition'GD_Weap_Pistol.Barrel.Pistol_Barrel_Dahl_Hornet',Manufacturers=((Manufacturer=None,DefaultWeightIndex=0),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Bandit',DefaultWeightIndex=0),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Dahl',DefaultWeightIndex=0),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Hyperion',DefaultWeightIndex=0),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Jakobs',DefaultWeightIndex=0),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Maliwan',DefaultWeightIndex=0),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Tediore',DefaultWeightIndex=0),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Torgue',DefaultWeightIndex=0),(Manufacturer=ManufacturerDefinition'GD_Manufacturers.Manufacturers.Vladof',DefaultWeightIndex=0)),MinGameStageIndex=0,MaxGameStageIndex=1,DefaultWeightIndex=0)))</code>
								</category>

							<category name="Greed">
								<category name="Barrel">
									<code profiles="default">set GD_Orchid_BossWeapons.Pistol.Pistol_Barrel_ScarletsGreed WeaponAttributeEffects ()</code>
									<code profiles="default">set GD_Orchid_BossWeapons.Pistol.Pistol_Barrel_ScarletsGreed ExternalAttributeEffects ()</code>
									<code profiles="default">set GD_Orchid_BossWeapons.Pistol.Pistol_Barrel_ScarletsGreed ZoomWeaponAttributeEffects ()</code>
									<code profiles="default">set GD_Orchid_BossWeapons.Pistol.Pistol_Barrel_ScarletsGreed ZoomExternalAttributeEffects ()</code>
									<code profiles="default">set GD_Orchid_BossWeapons.Pistol.Pistol_Barrel_ScarletsGreed AttributeSlotUpgrades ((SlotName="WeaponFireRate",GradeIncrease=-3,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="WeaponDamage",GradeIncrease=6,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="WeaponSpread",GradeIncrease=8,bActivateSlot=True))</code>
								</category>
								<category name="Material">
									<code profiles="default">set GD_Orchid_BossWeapons.ManufacturerMaterials.Mat_Jakobs_3_Greed AttributeSlotUpgrades ((SlotName="WeaponReloadSpeed",GradeIncrease=-3,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="WeaponDamage",GradeIncrease=19,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="WeaponZoomFOV",GradeIncrease=2,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="WeaponAccuracyImpulse",GradeIncrease=45,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="WeaponSpread",GradeIncrease=4,bActivateSlot=True),(SlotName="AccuracyRegen",GradeIncrease=5,bActivateSlot=True))</code>
									<code profiles="default">set GD_Orchid_BossWeapons.ManufacturerMaterials.Mat_Jakobs_3_Greed ExternalAttributeEffects ((AttributeToModify=AttributeDefinition'D_Attributes.GameplayAttributes.PlayerCriticalHitBonus',ModifierType=MT_PreAdd,BaseModifierValue=(BaseValueConstant=0.250000,BaseValueAttribute=None,InitializationDefinition=None,BaseValueScaleConstant=1.000000)))</code>
								</category>
